msg:Environment: Because the hotel is old, the sound insulation effect of the room is very poor. You can also hear shouts from other rooms in the early morning, which affects sleep.

Facilities: In terms of bathing - although the booked room has a shower, it is decorated with a bathtub underneath, which can be showered, but because the bathtub is too old, the water processing is slow, and the water at the feet overflows several times.
In terms of lighting - the lights in the room are controlled by a main switch. Because the facilities are old, you need to press many buttons to switch the lights, which is very inconvenient to operate.
Bedside table-Although the bedside table provides a charging cable for the mobile phone data cable, the charging can only be charged slowly. In addition, the setting of the bedside table without a socket is confusing.

Safety: The hotel elevator is not equipped with card swiping control, so people outside the hotel can also go up and down at will, and the safety aspect needs to be considered.

Hygiene: There is a musty smell in the hotel's aisles, elevators, and rooms. I don't know whether it is due to poor cleaning or the old and disrepaired hotel.

Sincerely raise the above questions for Dorsett Hotel. A good word of mouth requires actually good accommodation conditions, rather than blindly calling the front desk to ask for good reviews.

Accommodation is not recommended, and the price/performance ratio is not high, unless the above-mentioned needs are completely ignored.

msg:Before arriving in Shantou, I was still looking forward to this five-star hotel
Although it is expected that the hotel built in the 90s may be relatively old, but entering the door really breaks my bottom line

Room view:
First of all, the whole room is filled with a musty smell of disrepair, whether it is the carpet or the wallpaper, there is a yellowed old feeling
Secondly, I really can't accept why the hotel's bed faces the mirror, and the two beds face the mirror. Didn't the hotel design pay attention to this? ? Really unheard and unseen. And the design of the mirror cabinet and the placement of the lamps...it gives people an indescribable feeling...I feel panicked when I sleep at night

Room facilities:
There are only table lamps and a few floor lamps in the room. There is no ceiling lamp installed. The overall lighting is dark yellow, not bright, and feels very dark and depressing.
The bedside table does not have any rechargeable sockets, but only one charging cable. What kind of design is there for a double bed in a standard room with only one charging cable to charge a mobile phone? One person is charging and the other can only rely on power bank. Simply disregarding the needs of contemporary life
The hotel's bathroom is a very old design, there is no separate shower room, you need to stand in the bathtub to wash


health:
The upper part of one pillow exudes the smell of oily head, the middle part smells of disinfectant water, and the lower part smells of mold; the other pillow has a big nose and unknown dirt. It's really hard to imagine the sanitation of the room. Isn't the pillowcase cleaned in time? ?


wifi:
wifi is very slow! rather slow! Not even as good as my 5G


Cost performance:
The overall price/performance ratio is really low. Various fast hotels are emerging in an endless stream. The fast chain hotels can meet the needs of young people back then, ensuring a clean environment, smart systems, and cheap prices. Only relying on the reputation of the old brand does not follow the needs of the times, and the basic hygiene and environment are very rubbish! Really bad! ! At the same price or even lower price, you can completely get the experience of n steps higher!

I originally booked for two nights, but I got a refund for one night, and ran away early the next morning. If I hadn't checked in that night, I really didn't want to cause trouble for others, and I really couldn't stay at all.
